 lekin pramukh vipakshi dal bhartiya janata party (bhaajapa) ne aaropon kii nishpaksh jaanch kii maang kii

 team ne real estate kshetra kii pramukh company dlef dwaara wadra ko bina byaaj or bina kisi suraksha raashi ke 65 karod rupee kaa rin dene par sawalia nishaan khadaa kiya
 According to the team, with this money Vadra made crores of rupees
 kejariwal ne shuukravaar ko yahaan ek samvaadadaata sammelan main kaha, "dlef ne priyanka gandhi ke pati wadra ko pehle 65 karod rupee kaa rin diya

 unhone kaha, "robert wadra ne hajaaron karod rupee kii sampatti kharidi

 Vadra has bought seven DLF flats out of it
 kejariwal ke sahyogi evam prasiddh adhivaktaa prashanth bhushan ne kaha, "aakhir kyon dlef ne wadra ko bagaiyr rin va bagaiyr suraksha raashi ke yah rakam diya?" Prashant said on the basis of documents received from the Registrar of India, "vadra created five companies in 2007, whose director was for some time with his wife Priyanka Gandhi, though she later withdrew from it
 vartmaan main is company main wadra evam unki maa nideshak thim
 "he said that according to the balance sheet of these five companies, their capital is only fifty lakh rupees

 He said that DLF first gave cheap loans to Vadra's companies and then sold its properties for a few cents
 bhushan ne aarope lagaaya ki wadra ko sasti jameen dene ke kaaran dilli evam haryana kii sarkaron ne dlef ke liye bhoomi adhigrahan kiya

 " On the other hand, Congress spokesperson Manish Tiwari called these allegations a political trick of the worse

 wadra ne isamen se dlef ke saat flats kharide hai

 ' The government sent another notice to whatsapp today (thursday) asking for an effective solution to prevent the spread of fake and misleading messages (fake news)
 sarkaar ne company ko chetavanee di he ki afvaahon ke prasar main madhyam banane vaale bhi doshi maane jaaenge or mook darshak bane rahane par unhen bhi kanoonee karrwai kaa saamana karnaa padegaa
 Explain that the government has taken a tough stand on whatsapp after several cases of violence, including the killing of innocent persons by an angry mob due to spreading fake and misleading messages in the country
 sarkaar isse pehle bhi watsap ko is tarah kii khabaron evam sandeshon par roak lagane ke liye chetavanee de chuki he
 In a statement issued by the Ministry of Information Technology, "when rumors or falsified news are spread by bad elements, those who become media in such propaganda cannot avoid responsibility and accountability
" yadi ve mookadarshak bane rahete hai to unhen bhi in sandeshon kaa vaahak mana jayega or phir unhen aage kii kanoonee karrwai kaa saamana karnaa padegaa

 Roads made of plastic waste in Odisha
 2
 Profiles are being credited for making roads with plastic in the country using plastic
 Prof
 Rajagopalan Vasudevan
 72 varshiya padmashri vijeta vasudevan thiagaraj college of ejineering madurai ke dean hai
 He is also known as The Plastic Man
 inhone ek baar tivi par ek kaarykram main suna ki plastic pani main ghulata nahin he
 After this he became worried
 unhone chemistry lab main iskaa hal khojna shuru kiya
 In the year 2002, Prof
 vasudevan ne apane college kii sadak ko plastic se banaaya
 They used plastic carrybags, plastic cups, food chips and plastic packets of biscuits
 pro
 Vasudevan melted the plastic at 165 ° c and mixed it with bitumen and road making material
 phir isse sadak banaai gai
 Due to this, the road became so strong that the probability of its breakdown or deterioration was reduced to 1 percent
 ab desh ke kai shaharon main aisi sadaken bani hui hai
 Roads made of plastic are present in Kovilpatti, Kothamangalam, Madurai, Salem, Wellington, Chennai, Puducherry, Hindpur, Kolkata, Shimla, Thiruvananthapuram, Vadakara, Calicut, Jamshedpur and Kochi
